Normally, it costs about 50 yuan to recharge outside, so from this point of view, the cost performance is super high. If you are traveling short distances, those who drive trams can take a look here, it is worth a reference. And you can recharge for free during your stay, with no limit on the number of times; I recommend everyone to drive a tram to stay here;
